Visnu-Purana
Based on: The Critical Edition of the Viùõupuràõam,
critically edited by M. M. Pathak. Vadodara : Oriental Institute 1997-1999. 



Input by Peter Schreiner.



PLAIN TEXT VERSION




STRUCTURE OF REFERENCES:
ViP_n,nn.nn = number of aü÷a,adhyàya.verse
ViP_n,nn.nn*nn(:nn) = number of PRECEDING aü÷a,adhyàya.verse*insertion(:line [optional for insertions of more than one line]) 
ViP_n,nn.nn@n:nn = number of PRECEDING aü÷a,adhyàya.verse@appendix:line

/ = daõóa in metric parts
| = daõóa in prose parts
... = interlocutors
xxx = missing/illegible character
